NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
S. Annakili a female child born to Mr. Selvam on 5th April 1987 residing at 8-231/9-38, Nehruji Street, Sayalkudi,
Kadaladi Taluk, Ramanathapuram District has been living as a male after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery by
Dr. Vijay J. Ms. MRCS, Reg. No. 73897, Asst. Professor of plastic surgery, Mahatma Gandhi Medical College and Research
Institute, Puducherry-607 402. By this I, May be treated as a male and shall henceforth be known as S. ANISH.

Ramanathapuram,
27th June 2017.

S. ANNAKILI

A. Satheesh a male born to Arjunan. M on 8th July 1994 at 239, West Street, Samayan Kkuidkkadu, Okkanadu
Melaiyur Post, Orathanadu Taluk, Thanjavur-614 625, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment
surgery by Dr. P. Saravanan, Saravana Multi Specialty Hospital, 7A-Marudhupandiar Nagar, 4th Main Road, Narimedu,
Madurai-625 002. By this, I may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be known as A. SANAA SHASU

Thanjavur,
27th June 2017.

A. SATHEESH
